                return false;
            }

        function WindowKeyEvent(evt, flag) {
            s_ctrlPressed = evt.ctrlKey || evt.shiftKey || evt.altKey;
            //keyCode 13: Enter
            if (evt.keyCode == 13 && !(evt.target?.tagName == "TEXTAREA" || evt.target?.tagName == "A")) {
                evt.preventDefault();
                return false;
            }
            //keyCode 33: Page Up
            //keyCode 34: Page Down
            if ((evt.keyCode == 33 || evt.keyCode == 34) && evt.target?.tagName == "INPUT") {
                evt.preventDefault();
                return false;
            }
        }

        function OpenLink(link) {
            if (s_ctrlPressed) {
                return false;
            }
            document.location.href = link
            return false;
        }

        onload = function () {
            var _checker = document.getElementById("_HiddenFieldRefreshControl");

            if (_checker.value == "Refresh-Post-No") {
                _checker.value = "Refresh-Post-Yes";
            }
            else if (_checker.value == "Refresh-Post-Yes") {
                _checker.value = "Refresh-Post-No";
                location.reload(true);
            }
            else if (_checker.value == "Refresh-No") {
                _checker.value = "Refresh-Yes";
            }
            else if (_checker.value == "Refresh-Yes") {
                _checker.value = "Refresh-No";
                document.body.style.visibility = "hidden";
                location.href = location.href;
            }
            else {
            }
        }

        function ReportAdvanceOption() {
            var _dropDowns = document.getElementsByTagName("SELECT");
            var _advanceOption = null;

            if (_dropDowns != null) {
                for (var i = 0; i < _dropDowns.length; i++) {
                    var _dropDown = _dropDowns[i];
                    if (_dropDown.id.indexOf("_DropDownListReportOption", 0) != -1) {
                        _advanceOption = _dropDown;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }

            if (_advanceOption != null) {
                for (var i = 0; i < _advanceOption.options.length; i++) {
                    var _option = _advanceOption.options[i];
                    if (_option.value == "*ADVANCED OPTIONS*") {
                        _option.selected = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

function __doPostBack(eventTarget, eventArgument) {
    if (!theForm.onsubmit || (theForm.onsubmit() != false)) {
        theForm.__EVENTTARGET.value = eventTarget;
        theForm.__EVENTARGUMENT.value = eventArgument;
        theForm.submit();
    }
}

function JS_FormatDateTime(dateObj, dateOnly){    var _result = '';    var _value = '00' + (dateObj.getMonth() + 1);    _result += _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);    _value = '00' + dateObj.getDate();    _result += '/' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);    _value = dateObj.getFullYear();    _result += '/' + _value;    if(!dateOnly)    {        _value = '00' + dateObj.getHours();        _result += ' ' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);        _value = '00' + dateObj.getMinutes();        _result += ':' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);        _value = '00' + dateObj.getSeconds();        _result += ':' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);    }    return _result;}function JS_FormatDateTimeUTC(dateObj, dateOnly){    var _result = '';    var _value = '00' + (dateObj.getUTCMonth() + 1);    _result += _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);    _value = '00' + dateObj.getUTCDate();    _result += '/' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);    _value = dateObj.getUTCFullYear();    _result += '/' + _value;    if(!dateOnly)    {        _value = '00' + dateObj.getUTCHours();        _result += ' ' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);        _value = '00' + dateObj.getUTCMinutes();        _result += ':' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);        _value = '00' + dateObj.getUTCSeconds();        _result += ':' + _value.substr(_value.length - 2, 2);    }    return _result;}//]]>

<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
function JS_SubStringWithNewLineAs2Chars(inputValue, count){    var _lines = inputValue.split('\n');    var _result = '';    var _totalCount = 0;    for(var i = 0; i < _lines.length && _totalCount < count; i++)    {        if(_totalCount + _lines[i].length + 2 <= count)        {            _result += _lines[i] + '\n';            _totalCount += _lines[i].length + 2;        }        else if(_totalCount + _lines[i].length < count )        {            _result += _lines[i];            _totalCount += _lines[i].length + 2;        }        else        {            _result += _lines[i].substr(0, count - _totalCount);            _totalCount += (count - _totalCount);        }    }    return _result;}//]]>
</script>

//<![CDATA[
function JS_GetPosition(obj){    if (typeof(obj.offsetParent) != null)    {        var _sourceObj = obj;        for (var x = 0, y = 0; obj; obj = obj.offsetParent)        {            x += obj.offsetLeft;            y += obj.offsetTop;            if (obj != _sourceObj && obj != document.body && obj != document.documentElement)            {                x -= obj.scrollLeft;                y -= obj.scrollTop;            }        }        return { left: x, top: y, width: _sourceObj.offsetWidth, height: _sourceObj.offsetHeight, widthNoPadding: _sourceObj.clientWidth, heightNoPadding: _sourceObj.clientHeight};    }    else    {        return { left: obj.x, top: obj.y, width: obj.offsetWidth, height: obj.offsetHeight, widthNoPadding: obj.clientWidth, heightNoPadding: obj.clientHeight };    }}function JS_MoveItemInView(obj, xy){    var _scrollX = JS_ScrollLeft();    var _scrollY = JS_ScrollTop();    var _viewWidth = JS_ViewWidth();    var _viewHeight = JS_ViewHeight();    if(xy[0] < _scrollX)     {        _scrollX =  xy.left;    }    if(xy[0] + obj.offsetWidth > _scrollX + _viewWidth)     {        _scrollX +=  xy.left + obj.offsetWidth - (_scrollX + _viewWidth);    }    if(xy[1] < _scrollY)     {        _scrollY =  xy.top;    }    if(xy.top + obj.offsetHeight > _scrollY + _viewHeight)     {        _scrollY +=  xy.top + obj.offsetHeight - (_scrollY + _viewHeight);    }    window.scrollTo(_scrollX, _scrollY);}function JS_SetSubObjectPosition(obj, objSub){    JS_SetSubObjectPosition(obj, objSub, '');}function JS_SetSubObjectPosition(obj, objSub, align){    if(align == null)    {        align = '';    }    if(objSub == null || objSub.offsetWidth == null)    {        return;    }    if(align != '' && objSub.offsetWidth == 0)    {        setTimeout(function(){JS_SetSubObjectPosition(document.getElementById(obj.id), document.getElementById(objSub.id), align);}, 100);        return;    }    switch(align.toLowerCase())    {        case 'left':            objSub.style.position = 'absolute';            objSub.style.left = (objSub.offsetLeft - obj.clientWidth) + 'px';            break;        case 'right':            objSub.style.position = 'absolute';            objSub.style.left = (objSub.offsetLeft - objSub.offsetWidth) + 'px';            break;        case 'center':            objSub.style.position = 'absolute';            objSub.style.left = (objSub.offsetLeft - parseInt((obj.offsetWidth + objSub.offsetWidth) / 2, 10)) + 'px';            break;        default:            break;    }}//CONTROL NAME:TSClientCalendar

<script language="JavaScript">function TSListBox_FilterClear(listID){	document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcListFilter').value = '';    document.getElementById(listID + '_DstListFilter').value = '';	TSListBox_FilterOption(document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcListFilter'), listID);	TSListBox_FilterOption(document.getElementById(listID + '_DstListFilter'), listID);	document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcListCount').innerHTML = document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcList').options.length;    document.getElementById(listID + '_DstListCount').innerHTML = document.getElementById(listID + '_DstList').options.length;}function TSListBox_FilterOption(inputFilter, listID){	var srcList = document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcList');	var dstList = document.getElementById(listID + '_DstList');	var optionList = null;	var filterValue = inputFilter.value;	if(inputFilter.id.includes(srcList.id))	{	    optionList = srcList.options;	}	else	{	    optionList = dstList.options;	}	for(var i = 0; i < optionList.length; i++)	{	    if(optionList[i].hasAttribute('hidden'))	    {	        optionList[i].removeAttribute('hidden');	        optionList[i].removeAttribute('disabled');	    }	    if(filterValue != '')	    {	        if(!optionList[i].label.toUpperCase().includes(filterValue.toUpperCase()))	        {	            optionList[i].setAttribute('hidden', 'hidden');	            optionList[i].setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');	        }	    }	    else	    {	        if(optionList[i].hasAttribute('selected'))	        {	            optionList[i].removeAttribute('selected');	        }	    }	}	srcList.selectedIndex = -1;	dstList.selectedIndex = -1;}function TSListBox_ExecuteAddItem(listID, index){	var srcList = document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcList');	var dstList = document.getElementById(listID + '_DstList');	var selectedStateField = document.getElementById(listID + '_SelectedState');	var allStateField = document.getElementById(listID + '_AllState');	if (index == -1)	{		return;	}	var srcOption = srcList.options[index];	var dstOption = document.createElement("OPTION");	dstList.add(dstOption);	dstOption.text = srcOption.text;	dstOption.value = srcOption.value;	srcList.remove(index);	if (selectedStateField.value == '')	{		selectedStateField.value = dstOption.value;	}	else	{		selectedStateField.value = selectedStateField.value + ',' + dstOption.value;	}	TSListBox_SearchAndRemove(allStateField, dstOption.value);}function TSListBox_ExecuteRemoveItem(listID, index){	var srcList = document.getElementById(listID + '_DstList');    var dstList = document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcList');    var selectedStateField = document.getElementById(listID + '_SelectedState');    var allStateField = document.getElementById(listID + '_AllState');    if (index == -1)	{        return;	}    var srcOption = srcList.options[index];    var dstOption = document.createElement("OPTION");    dstList.add(dstOption);    dstOption.text = srcOption.text;    dstOption.value = srcOption.value;    srcList.remove(index);    if (allStateField.value == '')	{      allStateField.value = dstOption.value;	}    else	{      allStateField.value = allStateField.value + ',' + dstOption.value;	}    TSListBox_SearchAndRemove(selectedStateField, dstOption.value);}function TSListBox_AddItem(listID){	var srcList = document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcList');	while(srcList.selectedIndex != -1)	{	    TSListBox_ExecuteAddItem(listID, srcList.selectedIndex);	}	TSListBox_FilterClear(listID);}function TSListBox_AddAllItem(listID){	var srcList = document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcList');	var i = 0;	while(i < srcList.length)	{	    if(!srcList.options[i].hasAttribute('hidden'))	    {	        TSListBox_ExecuteAddItem(listID, i);	        i = 0;	    }	    else	    {	        i++;	    }	}	TSListBox_FilterClear(listID);}function TSListBox_RemoveItem(listID){	var dstList = document.getElementById(listID + '_DstList');	while(dstList.selectedIndex != -1)	{	    TSListBox_ExecuteRemoveItem(listID, dstList.selectedIndex);	}	TSListBox_FilterClear(listID);}function TSListBox_RemoveAllItem(listID){	var dstList = document.getElementById(listID + '_DstList');	var i = 0;	while(i < dstList.length)	{	    if(!dstList.options[i].hasAttribute('hidden'))	    {	        TSListBox_ExecuteRemoveItem(listID, i);	        i = 0;	    }	    else	    {	        i++;	    }	}	TSListBox_FilterClear(listID);}function TSListBox_FirstCount(listID){	document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcListCount').innerHTML = document.getElementById(listID + '_SrcList').options.length;    document.getElementById(listID + '_DstListCount').innerHTML = document.getElementById(listID + '_DstList').options.length;}function TSListBox_SearchAndRemove(stateField, item){    var newStateValue = '';    var counter = 0;    fields = stateField.value.split(',');    for (var i = 0; i< fields.length; i++)	{		if (fields[i] != item)		{            counter ++;            if (counter>1)                newStateValue = newStateValue + ',' + fields[i];            else                newStateValue = fields[i];        }   }    stateField.value = newStateValue;}</script>

//CONTROL NAME:TSGRidView
//DESIGNER:NIGEL H. LIN
//DESCRIPTION:
//CLIENT CLICK ASP.NET MENU
function TSMenu_HideItems(items)
{
    if (document.body.__oldOnClick)
	{
        document.body.onclick = document.body.__oldOnClick;
        document.body.__oldOnClick = null;
    }
    Menu_ClearInterval();
    if (!items || ((typeof(items.tagName) == "undefined") && (items instanceof Event)))
	{
        items = __rootMenuItem;
    }
    var table = items;
    if ((typeof(table) == "undefined") || (table == null) || !table.tagName || (table.tagName.toLowerCase() != "table"))
	{
        table = WebForm_GetElementByTagName(table, "TABLE");
    }
    if ((typeof(table) == "undefined") || (table == null) || !table.tagName || (table.tagName.toLowerCase() != "table"))
	{
        return;
    }
    var rows = table.rows ? table.rows : table.firstChild.rows;
    var isVertical = false;
    for (var r = 0; r < rows.length; r++)
	{
        if (rows[r].id)
		{
            isVertical = true;
            break;
        }
    }
    var i, child, nextLevel;
    if (isVertical)
	{
        for(i = 0; i < rows.length; i++)
		{
            if (rows[i].id)
			{
                child = WebForm_GetElementById(rows[i].id + "Items");
                if (child)
				{
                    TSMenu_HideItems(child);
                }
            }
            else if (rows[i].cells[0])
			{
                nextLevel = WebForm_GetElementByTagName(rows[i].cells[0], "TABLE");
                if (nextLevel)
				{
                    TSMenu_HideItems(nextLevel);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    else if (rows[0])
	{
        for(i = 0; i < rows[0].cells.length; i++)
		{
            if (rows[0].cells[i].id)
			{
                child = WebForm_GetElementById(rows[0].cells[i].id + "Items");
                if (child)
				{
                    TSMenu_HideItems(child);
                }
            }
            else
			{
                nextLevel = WebForm_GetElementByTagName(rows[0].cells[i], "TABLE");
                if (nextLevel)
				{
                    TSMenu_HideItems(rows[0].cells[i].firstChild);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if (items && items.id)
	{
        PopOut_Hide(items.id);
    }
}
function TSMenu_Collapse(item)
{
    TSMenu_SetRoot(item);
    if (__rootMenuItem)
	{
		TSMenu_HideItems();
    }
}
function TSMenu_Unhover(item)
{
    var node = (item.tagName.toLowerCase() == "td") ?
        item:
        item.cells[0];
    var nodeTable = WebForm_GetElementByTagName(node, "table");
    if (nodeTable.hoverClass)
	{
        WebForm_RemoveClassName(nodeTable, nodeTable.hoverClass);
    }
    node = nodeTable.rows[0].cells[0].childNodes[0];
    if (node.hoverHyperLinkClass)
	{
        WebForm_RemoveClassName(node, node.hoverHyperLinkClass);
    }
    TSMenu_Collapse(node);
}
var s_TSMenuActiveItem = null;
function TSMenuStaticClick(item, evt)
{
    JS_StopPropagation(evt);
    if(s_TSMenuActiveItem != null)
	{
	    TSMenu_Unhover(s_TSMenuActiveItem);
    }
    if(s_TSMenuActiveItem == item)
	{
	    s_TSMenuActiveItem = null;
	    return;
    }
    s_TSMenuActiveItem = item;
    Menu_HoverStatic(item);
}
var s_TSMenuActiveDynamicItem = null;
function TSMenuDynamicClick(item, evt)
{
    JS_StopPropagation(evt);
    if(s_TSMenuActiveDynamicItem != null)
	{
	    TSMenu_Unhover(s_TSMenuActiveDynamicItem);
        Menu_HoverStatic(s_TSMenuActiveItem);
    }
    s_TSMenuActiveDynamicItem = item;
    Menu_HoverDynamic(item);
}
function TSPopOut_Up(item, evt)
{
    JS_StopPropagation(evt);
    PopOut_Up(item);
}
function TSPopOut_Down(item, evt)
{
    JS_StopPropagation(evt);
    PopOut_Down(item);
}
function TSMenu_SetRoot(item)
{
    var newRoot = Menu_FindMenu(item);
    if (newRoot)
	{
        if (__rootMenuItem && __rootMenuItem != newRoot)
		{
            TSMenu_HideItems();
        }
        __rootMenuItem = newRoot;
    }
}
document.onclick = function(){TSMenu_CloseCheck();};
function TSMenu_CloseCheck()
{
    if(s_TSMenuActiveItem != null)
	{
	    TSMenu_Unhover(s_TSMenuActiveItem);
	    s_TSMenuActiveItem = null;
    }
}
Menu_HideItems=function(){};
</script>

    <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Table">
        <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">Q:&nbsp;&nbsp;</td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">HOW DO I CHANGE MY CALENDAR SETTINGS?</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">A:&nbsp;&nbsp;
            </td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">
                CLICK ON 'SHOW CONFIGURATION' TO SEE A LIST OF CONFIGURATION OPTIONS.<br />
                YOU CAN SELECT SPECIFIC BRANCHES WITH THE LISTBOX OR CLICK ON 'INCLUDE ALL MY BRANCHES' TO SEE ALL BRANCHES YOU ARE INCLUDED IN.<br />
                YOU CAN ALSO CHANGE WHICH CALENDAR ITEMS YOU WANT TO SHOW BY CLICKING ON THE CHECKBOXES NEXT TO THE ITEM OPTIONS.<br />
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td>&nbsp;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">Q:&nbsp;&nbsp;</td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">WHY DIDN'T MY CALENDAR SETTINGS SAVE?</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">A:&nbsp;&nbsp;
            </td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">
                TO SAVE YOUR CALENDAR SETTINGS, YOU MUST CLICK ON 'SET PREFERENCE' AFTER CHANGING YOUR CALENDAR SETTINGS THROUGH 'SHOW CONFIGURATION'.<br />
                CLICKING 'CONFIG CALENDAR' WILL ONLY SAVE THESE SETTINGS TEMPORARILY AND YOUR SAVED PREFERENCE CALENDAR SETTINGS WILL SHOW NEXT TIME YOU OPEN CALENDAR.<br />
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td>&nbsp;</td>
        </tr>
         <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">Q:&nbsp;&nbsp;</td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">WHAT DOES THE 'RESTORE DEFAULT' BUTTON DO?</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">A:&nbsp;&nbsp;
            </td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">CLICKING ON 'RESTORE DEFAULT' WILL OVERRIDE YOUR CALENDAR SETTINGS WITH THE SYSTEM'S DEFAULT CALENDAR CONFIGURATION.<br />
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td>&nbsp;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">Q:&nbsp;&nbsp;</td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Question">WHAT DOES THE ITEMS COLOR MEAN?</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
            <td align="right" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">A:&nbsp;&nbsp;
            </td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" class="FrequentlyAskedQuestions_Answer">INSIDE THE 'SHOW CONFIGURATION' PANEL EACH TYPE OF ITEM IS HIGHLIGHTED IN A COLOR, THIS COLOR IS USED TO MAP THE ITEM TYPE IN THE CALENDAR.<br />
            </td>
        </tr>
    </table>

function TSModalUpdating_Center(){    var _width = JS_ViewWidth();    var _height = JS_ViewHeight();    var _left = JS_ScrollLeft();    var _top = JS_ScrollTop();    if(_width == '100%')    {        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.width = _width;        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingBackGround').style.width = _width;        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingContainer').style.left = '50%';    }    else    {        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.width = _width + 'px';        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingBackGround').style.width = _width + _left + 'px';        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingContainer').style.left = parseInt((_width - parseInt(document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingContainer').style.width.replace('px', ''))) / 2) + _left + 'px';    }    if(_height == '100%')    {        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.height = _height;        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingBackGround').style.height = _height;        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingContainer').style.top = '50%';    }    else    {        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.height = _height + 'px';        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingBackGround').style.height = _height + _top + 'px';        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingContainer').style.top = parseInt((_height - parseInt(document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingContainer').style.height.replace('px', ''))) / 2) + _top + 'px';    }}function TSModalUpdating_Show(){    TSModalUpdating_Center();    document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.visibility = 'visible';    document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.display = 'block';    if(navigator.appName.toUpperCase().indexOf('MICROSOFT') != -1)    {        document.getElementById('TSModalUpdatingImage').src = 'images/loading.gif?' + JS_QueryTicket();    }    var _form = document.getElementsByTagName('form');    for(var i = 0; i < _form.length; i++)    {        _form[i].style.visibility = 'hidden';    }}function TSModalUpdating_Hide(){    var _form = window.document.getElementsByTagName('form');    for(var i = 0; i < _form.length; i++)    {        _form[i].style.visibility = 'visible';    }    window.document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.visibility = 'hidden';    window.document.getElementById('TSModalUpdating').style.display = 'none';}</script><div id='TSModalUpdating' style='display:none;position:absolute;width:100%;height:100%;top:0px;left:0px;'>    <div id='TSModalUpdatingBackGround' style='filter:Alpha(Opacity=40);-moz-opacity:0.4;opacity:0.4;width:100%;height:100%;background-color:#999999;position:absolute;z-index:2147483646;top:0px;left:0px;'>    </div>    <div id='TSModalUpdatingContainer' style='position:absolute;height:15px;width:145px;z-index:2147483647;'>    <img id='TSModalUpdatingImage' src='images/loading.gif'></div></div>

    <script language="javascript">
        let s_time = 0;
        let s_startTime = document.visibilityState === 'visible' ? Date.now() : undefined;


        JS_AddEvent(window, 'focus', function () {
            if (TSUpdatePanelControlsForce != null) {
                TSUpdatePanelControlsForce();
            }

            if (s_startTime === undefined) {
                s_startTime = Date.now();
            }
        });

        JS_AddEvent(window, 'blur', function () {
            s_ctrlPressed = false;

            s_time += Date.now() - s_startTime;
            s_startTime = undefined;
        });

        refreshTimer = function () {
            let _time = (s_startTime ? Date.now() - s_startTime : 0) + s_time;
            document.getElementById("_LabelTimer").textContent = `TIME ON PAGE: ${(_time / 1000 / 60).toFixed(0)}:${(_time / 1000 % 60).toFixed(0).padStart(2, '0')}`;
            setTimeout(refreshTimer, 1000);
        }
        refreshTimer();

        document.querySelectorAll('input[type="submit"]').forEach(element => {
            element.addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
                if (event.keyCode === 13) {
                    event.target.click();
                }
            });
            element.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
                if (event.ctrlKey || event.shiftKey || event.altKey) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    return false;
                }
            });
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('input[type=text], textarea').forEach(element => {
            element.setAttribute("enterkeyhint", "enter");
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('a[href*=default]:not([href^=javascript], [target=_blank])').forEach(element => {
            element.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
                if (event.ctrlKey) {
                    return;
                }
                if (event.shiftKey || event.altKey) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    return;
                }
                if (document.getElementById("MODAL")) {
                    closeModal();
                }
                TSModalUpdating_Show();
            })
        });
    </script>
